Rest In Peace Techno ğŸ˜”
I've been a fan of Techno for six years. I can't ever express how sad the entire community feels, and how wonderful person he was. For all of you who don't know, Techno donated to  many charities constantly, had a very unique and smart sense of humor, and a very unique way of talking about things. He was a humble, honest guy who was happy he was living "the dream" as he called it. He participated in many tournaments and events of the Minecraft community, and always loved his fandom, receiving fanart and things like that. When he informed us he had cancer, he was so positive about it (as he was with most things) that I didn't even imagine this had a chance of happening. I can only wish the best for his family, and be proud of how much he grew as a person and as a YouTuber in the years I've watched him constantly. He had this joke of doing an "elbow reveal" someday where he'd finally show us what his elbow looked like... And... If you see the picture in  02:03 I can only laugh at the fact that he probably chose to hide his elbow on purpose, just because of the meme, and because he didn't want the elbow reveal to be that way. He used to joke around in 2019 about what it would be like if he passed, and this was when he was a perfectly healthy guy who seemed to have so much time left. And for that, the message the community wants to share with all it's to hug and show that you care to those important to you NOW, and not wait because things can turn downhill very quickly, and even if the person remains positive and jokes about it, don't let that make you think everything will be okay.   Rest In Peace Techno, I'm so glad I've met you and I'm thankful for everything you did and wanted to do. Hugs for the family <3
